Materials Recovery Facility (C&D MRF) is a specialized facility designed to process materials generated from construction, renovation, and demolition activities.
to process materials generated from construction, renovation, and demolition activities. Under 62-701.200(24), F.A.C., construction and demolition debris are defined as
Under 62-701.200(24), F.A.C., construction and demolition debris are defined as discarded materials that are generally non-water soluble and non- hazardous,
discarded materials that are generally non-water soluble and non- hazardous, including steel, glass, brick, concrete, asphalt, pipe, gypsum wallboard, lumber,
including steel, glass, brick, concrete, asphalt, pipe, gypsum wallboard, lumber, and other materials commonly associated with structural construction or demolition.
